TSAB KYI RGYUD DU SKYES PA'I DGE SLONG TSUL

KHRIMS RGYAL MTSAN GYIS DAM PA'I CHOS LA GUS PAS RGYA GAR GYI
RGYAL PO PHUN SUM TSOGS PA'I DPAL GYI RGYAL MTSAN GYI DBANG PHYUG
GZHAN PAS CHES MTHO BA DANG LDAN PA RA MA P'A

LA'I RING LA THEG PA CHEN PO'I MDO SDE DAM PA'I CHOS DRAN PA NYE
BAR GZHAG PA ZHES BYA BA'I SHAS SHIG 'GYUR BA'I 'PHRO YONGS SU
RDZOGS PAR BYAS NAS BSGYUR BA'O,, ,,

SLAD KYIS ZHUS THUG LA NI, DGE BA'I BSHES GNYEN ZHANG BU GCIG PA
ZHES RAB TU GRAGS SHING SKYE RGU RNAMS SGROG PA YANG 'JIG RTEN PA
NI, RANG LA PHAN PA'I RGYU MTSAN GYIS RJOD PA DE

DAG RNAMS KYI GSHIS YIN PA'I PHYIR TE, SKYES BU DES NI, SEMS CAN
LA BU GCIG PA BZHIN DU DGONGS PAS SRAS GCIG PA'O, ,DES NI, THUGS
RJE CHEN PO DANG LDAN PA MTSON NO, ,CHOS


@355B LA GNAS PA RNAMS LA SHES RAB 'OD CES GRAGS PA YANG THEG
PA'I RIM PA DANG MTHUN PAR MKHYEN CING BDEN PA GNYIS LA SOGS PA'I
SGOR BSDU BAS MOS PA DANG, NGES PA DANG, MNGON DU

RTOGS SHING SHES NAS RANG DANG GZHAN GYI NYON MONGS PA DANG SHES
BYA'I SGRIB PA'I MUN PA 'JOMS PA'I 'OD MDZAD PA'I PHYIR TE, DES
NI, SHES RAB CHEN PO'I NGAD LDAN PA DANG, BDAG DANG

GZHAN GYI DON PHUN SUM TSOGS PA BSTAN TO, ,DAM PA'I SKYE BO DES
GROGS MDZAD NAS DGE SLONG TSUL KHRIMS RGYAL MTSAN NYID KYIS DAG
PAR BYAS SO, ,DE LTAR NA DANG PO'I GZHI 'GYUR DANG,

ZHU CHEN DANG, TSIG DON GYI 'BREL DPYAD PA DANG, ZHU CHUNG DANG,
YANG 'BREL DPYAD PA DANG LNGAR ZHUS SHING GTUGS TE GTAN LA PHAB
PA'O, ,DAM CHOS MDO SDE RIN CHEN THEG PA KUN GYI GZHI

DANG RTZA BA BCUD DU GYUR PA'I THEG CHEN DRAN GZHAG 'DI, ,LEGS
BSGYUR DNGOS DANG DE YI GROGS BYED THAMS CAD DANG NI NAM MKHA'I
MTHAS GTUGS 'GRO KUN DGE BA DRI MED KYIS, ,SRID NA

BDE SBYIN SKYABS GNAS RDZOGS PA'I BYANG CHUB 'BRAS LDAN SA YI
GNAS SKABS LJON SHING LO 'DAB PHUN TSOGS SHOG ,DANG POR TSE 'DI
BRJES NAS SANGS RGYAS ZHING DAG SKYE ZHING 'KHOR TSE GZHAN

LA PHAN PA 'BA' ZHIG BYED PAR SHOG ,BAM PO'I GRANGS NI, MA BCAD
DO, ,GZHUNG TSAD NI, STONG PHRAG SUM CU RTZA DRUG TU RGYA DPE
RANG LA BZHUGS SO, ,SHLOO KA SUM BRGYA LA BAM POR BYAS NA BRGYA
NYI SHU'O,, ,,
